1599 //
1600 // NxNgc::sMaterialPassHeader * p_u_pass = (NxNgc::sMaterialPassHeader *)&p_u_mat[um][1];

1627

1634  Mem::Region* region = heap->ParentRegion();
1635  OSReport( "%12s: %6dK %6dK %6dK %6d \n",
1636  heap->GetName(),

1638  heap->mFreeMem.m_count / 1024,
1639  region->MemAvailable() / 1024,
1640  heap->mUsedBlocks.m_count
1641  );
1642  }
1643  gDumpHeap = false;
1644  }

1702  // Clear to black with alpha of 124.
1703  // This is important as the shadow volume stuff uses the alpha channel as a stencil buffer.
1704  // With destination alpha, the RGBA channels each have 6 bits, so they are only accurate to multiples of 4.
1705  // To save having to copy the alpha map to a texture, we do a 2-pass full-screen polygon.
1706  // 1. And the alpha channel with 128. As it was set to 124, anything positive will have bit (128) set.
1707  // 2. Blend alpha with framebuffer.
1708 // NsDisplay::setBackgroundColor( (GXColor){0,0,0,124} );
1709  NsDisplay::setBackgroundColor( (GXColor){0,0,0,255} );

2377  // 2nd pad controls texture display.
2378  static int tick;
2379  static unsigned short last;
2380  unsigned short current = padData[1].button;
2381  unsigned short press = ( current ^ last ) & current;
2382  last = current;
2383 
2384  if ( press & ( PAD_BUTTON_UP | PAD_BUTTON_DOWN | PAD_BUTTON_X | PAD_BUTTON_Y ) )
2385  {
2386  tick = 0;
2387  }
2388 
2389 
2390  if ( current & ( PAD_BUTTON_UP | PAD_BUTTON_DOWN | PAD_BUTTON_X | PAD_BUTTON_Y ) )
2391  {
2392  if ( tick == 20 )
2393  {
2394  press |= current;
2395  }
2396  if ( ( ( ( tick - 20 ) % 2 ) == 0 ) && ( tick > 20 ) )
2397  {
2398  press |= current;
2399  }
2400 
2401  tick++;
2402  }
2403 
2404  if ( press & PAD_BUTTON_UP ) g_scroll_material++;
2405  if ( press & PAD_BUTTON_DOWN ) g_scroll_material--;
2406  if ( ( press & PAD_BUTTON_UP ) && ( current & PAD_BUTTON_B ) ) g_scroll_material+=99;
2407  if ( ( press & PAD_BUTTON_DOWN ) && ( current & PAD_BUTTON_B ) ) g_scroll_material-=99;
2408  if ( g_view_scene )
2409  {
2410  if ( g_scroll_material < 0 ) g_scroll_material = 0;
2411  if ( g_scroll_material > ( g_view_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_materials - 1 ) ) g_scroll_material = g_view_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_materials - 1;
2412  }
2413 
2414  if ( press & PAD_BUTTON_X ) g_view_object++;
2415  if ( press & PAD_BUTTON_Y ) g_view_object--;
2416  if ( g_view_object < 0 ) g_view_object = 0;
2417  if ( g_view_object > g_object ) g_view_object = g_object;
2418 
2419  if ( press & PAD_BUTTON_A )
2420  {
2421  if ( g_material == -1 )
2422  {
2423  g_material = g_scroll_material;
2424  }
2425  else
2426  {
2427  g_material = -1;
2428  }
2429  }
2430  if ( g_material != -1 )
2431  {
2432  g_material = g_scroll_material;
2433  }

2436  {

2484  if ( ( g_material >= 0 ) && ( g_material < g_view_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_materials ) )
2485  {
2486  // Draw material.
2487

2489 
2490  uint8 save_passes = p_mat->m_passes;
2491  p_mat->m_passes = ( g_passes == -1 ) ? p_mat->m_passes : ( g_passes + 1 );
2492 
2493  // Adjust mip to render.
2494  int mip_off[4] = { 0, 0, 0, 0 };
2495  {
2496  NxNgc::sMaterialPassHeader * p_pass = &g_view_scene->mp_material_pass[p_mat->m_pass_item];
2497  for ( int tex = 0; tex < p_mat->m_passes; tex++, p_pass++ )
2498  {
2499  if ( p_pass->m_texture.p_data )
2500  {
2501  for ( int mm = 0; mm < g_mip; mm++ )
2502  {
2503  int mw = p_pass->m_texture.p_data->ActualWidth >> mm;
2504  int mh = p_pass->m_texture.p_data->ActualHeight >> mm;
2505  mip_off[tex] += ( mw * mh ) >> 1;
2506  }
2507  p_pass->m_texture.p_data->pTexelData += mip_off[tex];
2508  p_pass->m_texture.p_data->pAlphaData += mip_off[tex];
2509  p_pass->m_texture.p_data->ActualWidth >>= g_mip;
2510  p_pass->m_texture.p_data->ActualHeight >>= g_mip;
2511  }
2512  }
2513  }
2514 
2515  multi_mesh( p_mat,
2516  &g_view_scene->mp_material_pass[p_mat->m_pass_item],
2517  true,
2518  true );
2519  p_mat->m_passes = save_passes;
2520  // Adjust mip back.
2521  {
2522  NxNgc::sMaterialPassHeader * p_pass = &g_view_scene->mp_material_pass[p_mat->m_pass_item];
2523  for ( int tex = 0; tex < p_mat->m_passes; tex++, p_pass++ )
2524  {
2525  if ( p_pass->m_texture.p_data )
2526  {
2527  p_pass->m_texture.p_data->pTexelData -= mip_off[tex];
2528  p_pass->m_texture.p_data->pAlphaData -= mip_off[tex];
2529  p_pass->m_texture.p_data->ActualWidth <<= g_mip;
2530  p_pass->m_texture.p_data->ActualHeight <<= g_mip;
2531  }
2532  }
2533  }

3554 
3555 CScene * CEngine::s_plat_create_scene(const char *p_name, CTexDict *p_tex_dict, bool add_super_sectors)
3556 {
3557  // Create scene class instance
3558  CNgcScene *p_Ngc_scene = new CNgcScene;
3559  CScene *p_new_scene = p_Ngc_scene;
3560  p_new_scene->SetInSuperSectors( add_super_sectors );
3561  p_new_scene->SetIsSky( false );
3562 
3563  // Create a new sScene so the engine can track assets for this scene.
3564  NxNgc::sScene *p_engine_scene = new NxNgc::sScene();
3565  p_Ngc_scene->SetEngineScene( p_engine_scene );
3566 
3567  return p_new_scene;
3568 }
3569 
3570 #define MemoryRead( dst, size, num, src ) memcpy(( dst ), ( src ), (( num ) * ( size ))); \
3571  ( src ) += (( num ) * ( size ))
3572 
3573 /******************************************************************/
3574 /* */
3575 /* */
3576 /******************************************************************/
3577 static int s_plat_scene_size( void *p_mem, CTexDict *p_tex_dict, bool add_super_sectors, bool is_sky, bool is_dictionary )
3578 {
3579  void * p_start = p_mem;
3580 
3581  // Setup pointer to actual data.
3582  NxNgc::sSceneHeader * p_scene_header = (NxNgc::sSceneHeader *)p_mem;
3583  unsigned int * p32 = (unsigned int *)&p_scene_header[1];
3584 
3585  // Setup material DL pointer.
3586  NxNgc::sMaterialDL * blend_dl = (NxNgc::sMaterialDL *)p32;
3587  NxNgc::sTextureDL * tex_dl = (NxNgc::sTextureDL *)&blend_dl[p_scene_header->m_num_blend_dls];
3588  unsigned char * p8 = (unsigned char *)&tex_dl[p_scene_header->m_num_materials];
3589 
3590  int bytes = ( p_scene_header->m_num_blend_dls * sizeof( NxNgc::sMaterialDL ) ) + ( p_scene_header->m_num_materials * sizeof( NxNgc::sTextureDL ) );
3591  int rounded_bytes = ( bytes + 31 ) & ~31;
3592  int pad_bytes = rounded_bytes - bytes;
3593 
3594  p8 = &p8[pad_bytes];
3595 
3596  // Assign blend dl pointers.
3597  for ( uint bdl = 0; bdl < p_scene_header->m_num_blend_dls; bdl++ )
3598  {
3599  p8 += blend_dl[bdl].m_dl_size;
3600  }
3601 
3602  // Assign texture dl pointers.
3603  for ( uint tdl = 0; tdl < p_scene_header->m_num_materials; tdl++ )
3604  {
3605  p8 += tex_dl[tdl].m_dl_size;
3606  }
3607  p32 = (unsigned int *)p8;
3608 
3609  // Point past pool data.
3610  NxNgc::sObjectHeader* p_data = (NxNgc::sObjectHeader*)&((char*)p32)[p_scene_header->m_num_pool_bytes];
3611 
3612  // Setup VC wibble data.
3613  NxNgc::sMaterialVCWibbleKeyHeader * p_key_header = (NxNgc::sMaterialVCWibbleKeyHeader *)p32;
3614  NxNgc::sMaterialVCWibbleKey * p_key = (NxNgc::sMaterialVCWibbleKey *)&p_key_header[1];
3615  for ( int vc = 0; vc < p_scene_header->m_num_vc_wibbles; vc++ )
3616  {
3617  p_key_header = (NxNgc::sMaterialVCWibbleKeyHeader *)&p_key[p_key_header->m_num_frames];
3618  p_key = (NxNgc::sMaterialVCWibbleKey *)&p_key_header[1];
3619  }
3620  p32 = (uint32 *)p_key_header;
3621 
3622  // Setup material header data.
3623  NxNgc::sMaterialHeader *material_header = (NxNgc::sMaterialHeader *)p32;
3624  p32 = (uint32 *)&material_header[p_scene_header->m_num_materials];
3625 
3626  // Setup UV wibble data.
3627  NxNgc::sMaterialUVWibble *uv_wibble = (NxNgc::sMaterialUVWibble *)p32;
3628  p32 = (uint32 *)&uv_wibble[p_scene_header->m_num_uv_wibbles];
3629 
3630  // Setup material pass data.
3631  NxNgc::sMaterialPassHeader *material_pass = (NxNgc::sMaterialPassHeader *)p32;
3632  p32 = (uint32 *)&material_pass[p_scene_header->m_num_pass_items];
3633 
3634  if ( p_scene_header->m_num_pos )
3635  {
3636  p32 = &((unsigned int *)p32)[p_scene_header->m_num_pos*3];
3637  }
3638 
3639  if ( p_scene_header->m_num_nrm )
3640  {
3641  p32 = &((unsigned int *)p32)[p_scene_header->m_num_nrm*3];
3642  }
3643 
3644  if ( p_scene_header->m_num_col )
3645  {
3646  p32 = &((unsigned int *)p32)[p_scene_header->m_num_col];
3647  }
3648 
3649  if ( p_scene_header->m_num_tex )
3650  {
3651  p32 = &((unsigned int *)p32)[p_scene_header->m_num_tex*2];
3652  }
3653 
3654  if ( p_scene_header->m_num_shadow_faces )
3655  {
3656  p32 = (unsigned int *)(&((unsigned short *)p32)[p_scene_header->m_num_shadow_faces*3]);
3657  p32 = (unsigned int *)(&((NxNgc::sShadowEdge *)p32)[p_scene_header->m_num_shadow_faces]);
3658  }
3659 
3660  for( uint s = 0; s < p_scene_header->m_num_objects; ++s )
3661  {
3662  int num_mesh = p_data->m_num_meshes;
3663 
3664  char * p_skin = (char *)&p_data[1];
3665  int nbytes = p_data->m_skin.num_bytes;
3666  NxNgc::sDLHeader* p_dl = (NxNgc::sDLHeader*)&p_skin[nbytes];
3667 
3668  for( int m = 0; m < num_mesh; ++m )
3669  {
3670  if ( p_dl->m_size )
3671  {
3672  p_dl = (NxNgc::sDLHeader*)&(((char *)&p_dl[1])[p_dl->m_size]);
3673  }
3674  }
3675 
3676  p_data = (NxNgc::sObjectHeader*)p_dl;
3677  }
3678 
3679  // Point up hierarchy.
3680  uint32 * p_h = (uint32 *)p_data;
3681  uint32 num_hobj = *p_h++;
3682 
3683  CHierarchyObject * p_end = (CHierarchyObject *)p_h;
3684 
3685  p_end = &p_end[num_hobj];
3686 
3687  return (int)p_end - (int)p_start;
3688 }
3689 
3690 /******************************************************************/
3691 /* */
3692 /* */
3693 /******************************************************************/
3694 static CScene * s_plat_load_scene_guts( void *p_mem, CTexDict *p_tex_dict, bool add_super_sectors, bool is_sky, bool is_dictionary )
3695 {
3696  if ( s_correctable ) gCorrectColor = true;
3697 
3698  CSector* pSector;
3699  CNgcSector* pNgcSector;
3700 
3701  // Create scene class instance.
3702  CScene *new_scene;
3703  if( add_super_sectors )
3704  {
3705  // Use default size sector table.
3706  new_scene = new CNgcScene();
3707  }
3708  else
3709  {
3710  // Use minimum size sector table.
3711  new_scene = new CNgcScene( 1 );
3712  }
3713 
3714  new_scene->SetInSuperSectors( add_super_sectors );
3715  new_scene->SetIsSky( is_sky );
3716 
3717  // Get a scene id from the engine.
3718  CNgcScene *p_new_ngc_scene = static_cast<CNgcScene *>( new_scene );
3719 
3720  // Create a new sScene so the engine can track assets for this scene.
3721  NxNgc::sScene *p_engine_scene = new NxNgc::sScene();
3722  p_new_ngc_scene->SetEngineScene( p_engine_scene );
3723 
3724  // Set the dictionary flag.
3725  p_engine_scene->m_is_dictionary = is_dictionary;
3726 
3727 
3728 
3729 //------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
3730 
3731  // Setup pointer to actual data.
3732  p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data = (NxNgc::sSceneHeader *)p_mem;
3733  unsigned int * p32 = (unsigned int *)&p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data[1];
3734 
3735  // Setup material DL pointer.
3736  Dbg_MsgAssert( p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_blend_dls < 256, ( "Too many (>255) unique material DLs (%d)\n", p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_blend_dls ) );
3737  p_engine_scene->mp_blend_dl = (NxNgc::sMaterialDL *)p32;
3738  p_engine_scene->mp_texture_dl = (NxNgc::sTextureDL *)&p_engine_scene->mp_blend_dl[p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_blend_dls];
3739  unsigned char * p8 = (unsigned char *)&p_engine_scene->mp_texture_dl[p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_materials];
3740 
3741  int bytes = ( p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_blend_dls * sizeof( NxNgc::sMaterialDL ) ) + ( p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_materials * sizeof( NxNgc::sTextureDL ) );
3742  int rounded_bytes = ( bytes + 31 ) & ~31;
3743  int pad_bytes = rounded_bytes - bytes;
3744 
3745  p8 = &p8[pad_bytes];
3746 
3747  // Assign blend dl pointers.
3748  for ( uint bdl = 0; bdl < p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_blend_dls; bdl++ )
3749  {
3750  p_engine_scene->mp_blend_dl[bdl].mp_dl = p8;
3751  p8 += p_engine_scene->mp_blend_dl[bdl].m_dl_size;
3752  }
3753 
3754  // Assign texture dl pointers.
3755  for ( uint tdl = 0; tdl < p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_materials; tdl++ )
3756  {
3757  p_engine_scene->mp_texture_dl[tdl].mp_dl = p8;
3758  p8 += p_engine_scene->mp_texture_dl[tdl].m_dl_size;
3759  }
3760  p32 = (unsigned int *)p8;
3761 
3762  // Point past pool data.
3763  NxNgc::sObjectHeader* p_data = (NxNgc::sObjectHeader*)&((char*)p32)[p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_pool_bytes];
3764 
3765  // Setup VC wibble data.
3766  p_engine_scene->mp_vc_wibble = (NxNgc::sMaterialVCWibbleKeyHeader *)p32;
3767  NxNgc::sMaterialVCWibbleKeyHeader * p_key_header = p_engine_scene->mp_vc_wibble;
3768  NxNgc::sMaterialVCWibbleKey * p_key = (NxNgc::sMaterialVCWibbleKey *)&p_key_header[1];
3769  for ( int vc = 0; vc < p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_vc_wibbles; vc++ )
3770  {
3771  p_key_header = (NxNgc::sMaterialVCWibbleKeyHeader *)&p_key[p_key_header->m_num_frames];
3772  p_key = (NxNgc::sMaterialVCWibbleKey *)&p_key_header[1];
3773  }
3774  p32 = (uint32 *)p_key_header;
3775 
3776  // Setup material header data.
3777  p_engine_scene->mp_material_header = (NxNgc::sMaterialHeader *)p32;
3778  p32 = (uint32 *)&p_engine_scene->mp_material_header[p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_materials];
3779 
3780  // Setup UV wibble data.
3781  p_engine_scene->mp_uv_wibble = (NxNgc::sMaterialUVWibble *)p32;
3782  p32 = (uint32 *)&p_engine_scene->mp_uv_wibble[p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_uv_wibbles];
3783 
3784  // Setup material pass data.
3785  p_engine_scene->mp_material_pass = (NxNgc::sMaterialPassHeader *)p32;
3786  p32 = (uint32 *)&p_engine_scene->mp_material_pass[p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_pass_items];
3787 
3788  // Setup material data texture pointers.
3789  NxNgc::sMaterialHeader * p_mat = p_engine_scene->mp_material_header;
3790  for ( unsigned int lp = 0; lp < p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_materials; lp++ )
3791  {
3792  p_mat->m_alpha_cutoff = p_mat->m_alpha_cutoff >= 128 ? 255 : p_mat->m_alpha_cutoff * 2;
3793  // Need to compensate for possible errors in alpha map.
3794 // int cut = (int)p_mat->m_alpha_cutoff - 16;
3795 // if ( cut < 0 ) cut = 0;
3796 // p_mat->m_alpha_cutoff = cut;
3797 
3798  // Setup texture pointer.
3799  NxNgc::sMaterialPassHeader * p_pass = &p_engine_scene->mp_material_pass[p_mat->m_pass_item];
3800 
3801  // Copy base pass blend mode to material.
3802  p_mat->m_base_blend = p_pass->m_blend_mode;
3803 
3804  for ( int pass = 0; pass < p_mat->m_passes; pass++ )
3805  {
3806  // If textured, resolve texture checksum...
3807  Nx::CNgcTexture *p_ngc_texture = static_cast<Nx::CNgcTexture*>( p_tex_dict->GetTexLookup()->GetItem( p_pass->m_texture.checksum ) );
3808  p_pass->m_texture.p_data = ( p_ngc_texture ) ? p_ngc_texture->GetEngineTexture() : NULL;
3809 
3810  // Temp HACK
3811 // p_pass->m_k = (1<<8);
3812 // p_pass->m_u_tile = (1<<12);
3813 // p_pass->m_v_tile = (1<<12);
3814 // p_pass->m_uv_enabled = 0;
3815 // p_pass->m_uv_mat[0] = (1<<12);
3816 // p_pass->m_uv_mat[1] = 0;
3817 // p_pass->m_uv_mat[2] = 0;
3818 // p_pass->m_uv_mat[3] = 0;
3819 
3820 
3821 
3822 
3823 
3824 
3825 
3826 // if ( p_pass->m_texture.checksum && !p_ngc_texture )
3827 // {
3828 // OSReport( "Failed to hook up texture!!!!!!!!!!! %08x\n", p_pass->m_texture.checksum );
3829 // }
3830 
3831 // // Adjust K value.
3832 // p_pass->m_mip_k += 8;
3833 
3834  // Switch color values.
3835 // u8 r;
3836 // u8 g;
3837 // u8 b;
3838 // u8 a;
3839 // r = p_pass->m_color.r;
3840 // g = p_pass->m_color.g;
3841 // b = p_pass->m_color.b;
3842 // a = p_pass->m_color.a;
3843 //
3844 // p_pass->m_color.r = b;
3845 // p_pass->m_color.g = g;
3846 // p_pass->m_color.b = r;
3847 // p_pass->m_color.a = a;
3848 
3849 // p_pass->m_color.a = 255;
3850 
3851 // p_pass->m_alpha_fix = ( p_pass->m_alpha_fix ) >= 128 ? 255 : p_pass->m_alpha_fix * 2;
3852 
3853  // Next pass structure.
3854  ++p_pass;
3855  }
3856 
3857  // Scan texture DL and patch texture address pointers.
3858  // Search for SetMode0/1 SetImage0/1/2/3.
3859  NxNgc::sTextureDL * p_dl = &p_engine_scene->mp_texture_dl[lp];
3860  p_pass = &p_engine_scene->mp_material_pass[p_mat->m_pass_item];
3861 
3862 // int search_size = ( p_dl->m_dl_size > ((5*5)+4) ) ? p_dl->m_dl_size - ((5*5)+4) : 0;
3863 
3864 // for ( int s = 0; s < search_size ; s++ )
3865  //for ( int s = 0; s < (int)p_dl->m_dl_size ; s++ )
3866 
3867  GX::ResolveDLTexAddr( p_dl, p_pass, p_mat->m_passes );
3868 
3869 // GX::begin( p_dl->mp_dl, p_dl->m_dl_size );
3870 // multi_mesh( p_mat, p_pass, true, true );
3871 // p_dl->m_dl_size = GX::end();
3872 
3873  ++p_mat;
3874  }
3875 
3876  // Setup vertex data.
3877  p_engine_scene->mp_pos_pool = NULL;
3878  p_engine_scene->mp_nrm_pool = NULL;
3879  p_engine_scene->mp_col_pool = NULL;
3880  p_engine_scene->mp_tex_pool = NULL;
3881 
3882  if ( p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_pos )
3883  {
3884  p_engine_scene->mp_pos_pool = (float *)p32;
3885  p32 = &((unsigned int *)p32)[p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_pos*3];
3886  }
3887 
3888  if ( p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_col )
3889  {
3890  p_engine_scene->mp_col_pool = (unsigned int *)p32;
3891  p32 = &((unsigned int *)p32)[p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_col];
3892  }
3893 
3894  if ( p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_tex )
3895  {
3896  p_engine_scene->mp_tex_pool = (s16 *)p32;
3897  p32 = (unsigned int *)&p_engine_scene->mp_tex_pool[p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_tex*2];
3898  }
3899 
3900  if ( p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_nrm )
3901  {
3902  p_engine_scene->mp_nrm_pool = (s16 *)p32;
3903  p32 = (unsigned int*)&p_engine_scene->mp_nrm_pool[p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_nrm*3];
3904  }
3905 
3906  if ( p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_shadow_faces )
3907  {
3908  p_engine_scene->mp_shadow_volume_mesh = (uint16*)p32;
3909  p32 = (unsigned int *)(&((unsigned short *)p32)[p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_shadow_faces*3]);
3910  p_engine_scene->mp_shadow_edge = (NxNgc::sShadowEdge *)p32;
3911  p32 = (unsigned int *)(&((NxNgc::sShadowEdge *)p32)[p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_shadow_faces]);
3912  }
3913 
3914  // Calculate radius.
3915  p_engine_scene->m_sphere[X] = 0.0f;
3916  p_engine_scene->m_sphere[Y] = 0.0f;
3917  p_engine_scene->m_sphere[Z] = 0.0f;
3918  p_engine_scene->m_sphere[W] = 0.0f;
3919 
3920  for ( uint32 lp = 0; lp < p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_pos; lp++ )
3921  {
3922  NsVector v;
3923  v.x = p_engine_scene->mp_pos_pool[(lp*3)+0];
3924  v.y = p_engine_scene->mp_pos_pool[(lp*3)+1];
3925  v.z = p_engine_scene->mp_pos_pool[(lp*3)+2];
3926  float l = v.length();
3927 
3928  if ( l > p_engine_scene->m_sphere[W] ) p_engine_scene->m_sphere[W] = l;
3929  }
3930 
3931  // Setup display list pointer.
3932  p_engine_scene->mp_dl = (NxNgc::sDLHeader *)&(((char*)&p_data[1])[p_data->m_skin.num_bytes]);
3933 
3934  for( uint s = 0; s < p_engine_scene->mp_scene_data->m_num_objects; ++s )
3935  {
3936  // Create a new sector to hold the incoming details.
3937  pSector = p_new_ngc_scene->CreateSector();
3938  pNgcSector = static_cast<CNgcSector*>( pSector );
3939 
3940  // Generate a hanging geom for the sector, used for creating level objects etc.
3941  CNgcGeom *p_Ngc_geom = new CNgcGeom();
3942  p_Ngc_geom->SetScene( p_new_ngc_scene );
3943  pNgcSector->SetGeom( p_Ngc_geom );
3944 
3945  // Prepare CNgcGeom for receiving data.
3946  p_Ngc_geom->InitMeshList();
3947 
3948  // Load sector data.
3949  p_data = pNgcSector->LoadFromFile( p_data );
3950  new_scene->AddSector( pSector );
3951 
3952 // if( ( p_data = pNgcSector->LoadFromFile( p_file, p_data ) ) )
3953 // {
3954 // new_scene->AddSector( pSector );
3955 // }
3956  }
3957 
3958  // At this point we can process any scaling that may need to be applied to the positions.
3959  if ( p_engine_scene->mp_dl->mp_object_header->m_skin.p_data )
3960  {
3961  NxNgc::ApplyMeshScaling( p_engine_scene->mp_dl->mp_object_header );
3962  }
3963 
3964  // Point up hierarchy.
3965  uint32 * p_h = (uint32 *)p_data;
3966  uint32 num_hobj = *p_h++;
3967 
3968  if ( num_hobj )
3969  {
3970  p_engine_scene->mp_hierarchyObjects = (CHierarchyObject *)p_h;
3971  p_engine_scene->m_numHierarchyObjects = num_hobj;
3972  //p32 = (uint32 *)&p_engine_scene->mp_hierarchyObjects[num_hobj];
3973 
3974 // p_engine_scene->mp_hierarchyObjects = new CHierarchyObject[num_hobj];
3975 //
3976 // File::Read( p_engine_scene->mp_hierarchyObjects, sizeof( CHierarchyObject ), num_hobj, p_file );
3977 //
3978 // p_engine_scene->m_numHierarchyObjects = num_hobj;
3979 
3980  // Fix up hierarchical object sphere.
3981  Lst::HashTable< Nx::CSector > *p_sector_list = new_scene->GetSectorList();
3982  if( p_sector_list )
3983  {
3984  p_sector_list->IterateStart();
3985  Nx::CSector *p_sector = p_sector_list->IterateNext();
3986  while( p_sector )
3987  {
3988  pNgcSector = static_cast<CNgcSector*>( p_sector );
3989  CNgcGeom *p_Ngc_geom = static_cast<CNgcGeom *>( pNgcSector->GetGeom() );
3990 
3991  Lst::Head< NxNgc::sMesh > *p_mesh_list = p_Ngc_geom->GetMeshList();
3992  int num_mesh = p_mesh_list->CountItems();
3993  if (num_mesh)
3994  {
3995  Lst::Node< NxNgc::sMesh > *mesh = p_mesh_list->GetNext();
3996  mesh->GetData()->mp_dl->mp_object_header->m_sphere[W] *= 2.0f;
3997  }
3998  p_sector = p_sector_list->IterateNext();
3999  }
4000  }
4001  }
4002 
4003  if ( s_correctable ) gCorrectColor = false;
4004 
4005  return new_scene;

4129 //
4130 // return new_scene;
4131 }

4133 /******************************************************************/
4134 /* */
4135 /* */
4136 /******************************************************************/
4137 CScene *CEngine::s_plat_load_scene_from_memory( void *p_mem, CTexDict *p_tex_dict, bool add_super_sectors, bool is_sky, bool is_dictionary )
4138 {
4139  int size = s_plat_scene_size( p_mem, p_tex_dict, add_super_sectors, is_sky, is_dictionary );
4140 
4141  int mem_available;
4142  bool need_to_pop = false;
4143  if ( g_in_cutscene )
4144  {
4145  Mem::Manager::sHandle().PushContext( Mem::Manager::sHandle().FrontEndHeap() );
4146  mem_available = Mem::Manager::sHandle().Available();
4147  if ( size < ( mem_available - ( 40 * 1024 ) ) )
4148  {
4149  need_to_pop = true;
4150  }
4151  else
4152  {
4153  Mem::Manager::sHandle().PopContext();
4154  Mem::Manager::sHandle().PushContext( Mem::Manager::sHandle().ThemeHeap() );
4155  mem_available = Mem::Manager::sHandle().Available();
4156  if ( size < ( mem_available - ( 5 * 1024 ) ) )
4157  {
4158  need_to_pop = true;
4159  }
4160  else
4161  {
4162  Mem::Manager::sHandle().PopContext();
4163  Mem::Manager::sHandle().PushContext( Mem::Manager::sHandle().ScriptHeap() );
4164  mem_available = Mem::Manager::sHandle().Available();
4165  if ( size < ( mem_available - ( 40 * 1024 ) ) )
4166  {
4167  need_to_pop = true;
4168  }
4169  else
4170  {
4171  Mem::Manager::sHandle().PopContext();
4172  }
4173  }
4174  }
4175  }
4176 
4177  Mem::Manager::sHandle().BottomUpHeap()->PushAlign( 32 );
4178  char * p_scene_data = new char[size];
4179  Mem::Manager::sHandle().BottomUpHeap()->PopAlign();
4180 
4181  if ( need_to_pop )
4182  {
4183  Mem::Manager::sHandle().PopContext();
4184  }
4185 
4186  memcpy( p_scene_data, p_mem, size );
4187  DCFlushRange( p_scene_data, size );
4188 
4189  return s_plat_load_scene_guts( p_scene_data, p_tex_dict, add_super_sectors, is_sky, is_dictionary );
4190 }
4191 
4192 /******************************************************************/
4193 /* */
4194 /* */
4195 /******************************************************************/
4196 CScene* CEngine::s_plat_load_scene( const char *p_name, CTexDict *p_tex_dict, bool add_super_sectors, bool is_sky, bool is_dictionary )
4197 {
4198  Dbg_Message( "loading scene from file %s\n", p_name );
4199 
4200  // Open the scene file.
4201  char gdname[128];
4202  sprintf( gdname, "%s", p_name );
4203  void* p_gd_file = File::Open( gdname, "rb" );
4204  if( !p_gd_file )
4205  {
4206  Dbg_MsgAssert( p_gd_file, ( "Couldn't open scene file %s\n", gdname ));
4207  if ( s_correctable ) gCorrectColor = false;
4208  return NULL;
4209  }
4210 
4211  // Read all data.
4212  int size = File::GetFileSize( p_gd_file );
4213  Mem::Manager::sHandle().BottomUpHeap()->PushAlign( 32 );
4214  char * p_scene_data = new char[size];
4215  Mem::Manager::sHandle().BottomUpHeap()->PopAlign();
4216  File::Read( p_scene_data, size, 1, p_gd_file );
4217 
4218  File::Close( p_gd_file );
4219 
4220  DCFlushRange( p_scene_data, size );
4221  return s_plat_load_scene_guts( p_scene_data, p_tex_dict, add_super_sectors, is_sky, is_dictionary );
4222 }

4237 /******************************************************************/
4238 /* */
4239 /* */
4240 /******************************************************************/
4241 bool CEngine::s_plat_unload_scene( CScene *p_scene )
4242 {
4243  Dbg_MsgAssert( p_scene,( "Trying to delete a NULL scene" ));
4244 
4245  CNgcScene *p_ngc_scene = (CNgcScene*)p_scene;
4246 
4247  // Ask the engine to remove the associated meshes for each sector in the scene.
4248  p_ngc_scene->DestroySectorMeshes();
4249 
4250  // Get the engine specific scene data and pass it to the engine to delete.
4251  NxNgc::DeleteScene( p_ngc_scene->GetEngineScene());
4252  p_ngc_scene->SetEngineScene( NULL );
4253 
4254  return true;
4255 }

4292 CMesh* CEngine::s_plat_load_mesh( const char* pMeshFileName, Nx::CTexDict* pTexDict, uint32 texDictOffset, bool isSkin, bool doShadowVolume )
4293 {
4294  s_correctable = false;
4295  // Load the scene.
4296  Nx::CScene *p_scene = Nx::CEngine::s_plat_load_scene( pMeshFileName, pTexDict, false, false, false );
4297  p_scene->SetID(Script::GenerateCRC( pMeshFileName )); // store the checksum of the scene name
4298  p_scene->SetTexDict( pTexDict );
4299  p_scene->PostLoad( pMeshFileName );
4300 
4301  // Disable any scaling.
4302  NxNgc::DisableMeshScaling();
4303 
4304  CNgcMesh *pMesh = new CNgcMesh( pMeshFileName );
4305  Nx::CNgcScene *p_Ngc_scene = static_cast<Nx::CNgcScene*>( p_scene );
4306  pMesh->SetScene( p_Ngc_scene );
4307  pMesh->SetTexDict( pTexDict );
4308  s_correctable = true;
4309  return pMesh;
4310 }

4312 /******************************************************************/

4314 /* */
4315 /******************************************************************/
4316 CMesh* CEngine::s_plat_load_mesh( uint32 id, uint32 *p_model_data, int model_data_size, uint8 *p_cas_data, Nx::CTexDict* pTexDict, uint32 texDictOffset, bool isSkin, bool doShadowVolume )
4317 {
4318  // Convert the id into a usable string.
4319  Dbg_Assert( id > 0 );
4320  char id_as_string[16];
4321  sprintf( id_as_string, "%d\n", id );
4322 
4323  // Load the scene.
4324  Nx::CScene *p_scene = Nx::CEngine::s_plat_load_scene_from_memory( p_model_data, pTexDict, false, false, false );
4325 
4326  // Store the checksum of the scene name.
4327  p_scene->SetID( Script::GenerateCRC( id_as_string ));
4328 
4329  p_scene->SetTexDict( pTexDict );
4330  p_scene->PostLoad( id_as_string );
4331 
4332  // Disable any scaling.
4333  NxNgc::DisableMeshScaling();
4334 
4335  CNgcMesh *pMesh = new CNgcMesh();
4336 
4337  // Set CAS data for mesh.
4338  pMesh->SetCASData( p_cas_data );
4339 
4340  Nx::CNgcScene *p_Ngc_scene = static_cast<Nx::CNgcScene*>( p_scene );
4341  pMesh->SetScene( p_Ngc_scene );
4342  pMesh->SetTexDict( pTexDict );
4343  return pMesh;
4344 }

4690 /******************************************************************/
4691 /* */
4692 /* */
4693 /******************************************************************/
4694 void CEngine::s_plat_set_letterbox( bool letterbox )
4695 {
4696  // Letterbox mode is designed for use on a regular 4:3 screen.
4697  // It should use the same, wider viewing angle as for widescreen mode, but shrink the resultant image down
4698  // vertically by 25%.
4699  if( letterbox )
4700  {
4701  if( NxNgc::EngineGlobals.letterbox_active == false )
4702  {
4703  // Need to adjust the screen y offset and multiplier to ensure sprites are scaled properly for this mode.
4704 // NxNgc::EngineGlobals.screen_conv_y_offset += ( NxXbox::EngineGlobals.backbuffer_height / 4 ) / 2;
4705 // NxNgc::EngineGlobals.screen_conv_y_multiplier = 0.75f;
4706  NxNgc::EngineGlobals.letterbox_active = true;
4707  }
4708  }
4709  else
4710  {
4711  if( NxNgc::EngineGlobals.letterbox_active == true )
4712  {
4713  // Restore the screen y offset and multiplier.
4714 // NxNgc::EngineGlobals.screen_conv_y_offset -= ( NxXbox::EngineGlobals.backbuffer_height / 4 ) / 2;
4715 // NxNgc::EngineGlobals.screen_conv_y_multiplier = 1.0f;
4716  NxNgc::EngineGlobals.letterbox_active = false;
4717  }
4718  }
4719 }
